speed of sound is about 1,220 km/h (760 mph) represents a Mach number of 1. The same speed in the stratosphere would correspond to a Mach number of 1.16, because of differences in density, pressure, and temperature higher up in the sky. <o:p></o:p></span></span><br />\n<span style=\"color: red;\"><o:p></o:p></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-size: 11pt; line-height: 115%; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;\">Sound</span><span style=\"font-size: 11pt; line-height: 115%;\"> propagates through air or other mediums as a<span style=\"font-size: x-large;\"> longitudinal wave</span> in which the mechanical vibration constituting the wave occurs along the direction of propagation of the wave. <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>S<span style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;\">ound</span> wave propagating as layers of air \u201cpush\u201d and \u201cpull\u201d .<o:p></o:p></span><br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\"><span class=\"querybold\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;;\">Alternating compressions and rarefactions or regions of high pressure and low pressure, moving at a certain speed. </span></span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><o:p></o:p></span></div><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-margin-top-alt: auto;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">A <span style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;\">sound</span> wave with a frequency of 20 hertz would have a period of 0.05 second (<i>i.e.,</i> 20 wavelengths/second \u00d7 0.05 second/wavelength = 1), while a <span style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;\">sound</span> wave of 20 kilohertz would have a period of 0.00005 second (20,000 wavelengths/second \u00d7 0.00005 second/wavelength = 1). Between 20 hertz and 20 kilohertz lies the frequency range of hearing for humans<a href=\"http://www.blogger.com/\" name=\"527151.hook\"></a>. <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>The physical property of frequency is perceived physiologically as pitch<a href=\"http://www.blogger.com/\" name=\"527152.hook\"></a>, so that the higher the frequency, the higher the perceived pitch. conservation an important part of the debate over climate change&nbsp;and the replacement of non-renewable resources&nbsp;with renewable energy. It is a buzz term the ships management must be familiar with. We we take it seriously and seek active feedback from shipstaff.</span><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; tab-stops: 45.8pt 91.6pt 137.4pt 183.2pt 229.0pt 274.8pt 320.6pt 366.4pt 412.2pt 458.0pt 503.8pt 549.6pt 595.4pt 641.2pt 687.0pt 732.8pt; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; tab-stops: 45.8pt 91.6pt 137.4pt 183.2pt 229.0pt 274.8pt 320.6pt 366.4pt 412.2pt 458.0pt 503.8pt 549.6pt 595.4pt 641.2pt 687.0pt 732.8pt; text-align: justify;\"><span lang=\"EN\" style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-ansi-language: EN; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Due to inefficiencies such as friction, heat loss, and other factors, thermal efficiencies are typically much less that 100%. For example, a typical gasoline automobile engine operates at around 25% thermal efficiency</span><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: 12.0pt;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><br />\nIt is the our policy to conserve energy, thus preserving resources and reducing expenses. It is a policy to do predictive maintenance of all fuel consumers&nbsp;&nbsp;and to use genuine spare parts while overhauling ships machinery.<br />\n<br />\nThe company\u2019s Energy Conservation Policy applies to all aspects of operation and includes all technical, operational and organizational personnel.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: 12.0pt;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><br />\n</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; text-align: justify;\"><a href=\"\" name=\"Heading29\"></a><b><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Technical Measures</span></b><span style=\"color: black; margin-bottom: 0in; text-align: justify;\"><b><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><br />\n</span></b></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Adjust autopilot controls based on actual sea conditions to prevent unnecessary working of rudder and large helm movements which increases propeller slip , or poor steering which increases the distance.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">When the difference between propeller speed and GPS speed becomes excessive master to reduce ships speed.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Understand black colour is a good absorber and a good radiator and vice versa or silver color.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Maintain all company equipment in an efficient working condition without leaks.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Run Framo power pack at 15 Bars system pressure above the highest consumer , or energy is wasted as heat.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Maintain all air filters clean.&nbsp;<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Reduce the consumption of fuel (M.D.O. &amp; H.F.O.) by maintaining the main engine, the turbochargers&nbsp;&nbsp;and all auxiliary machinery in a predictive and proactive manner.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Reduce lubricating oil and cylinder oil consumption. Worn out machinery should be replaced in good time and clearances maintained in accordance with manufacturer\u2019s instructions. Follow a predictive maintenance programme.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Use optimal ship\u2019s speed dependent upon the weather and sea conditions and the ships draft&nbsp;<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Eliminate all water, oil, air and steam leaks. All valves and pipes should be maintained in a planned and co-ordinated manner.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Reduce the consumption of electrical power during day and night by all appropriate means. Lights to be put on only when required.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Undertake quality repairs using genuine spares.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Reduce loss of heat and unnecessary firing of boiler by lagging lines and ensuring only water comes back in the return line to engine room, not steam.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Lights are focused and used in an optimum manner.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Maintain economizer so that firing of auxiliary boiler , dumping of steam and wastage of fuel is avoided. Soot must be blown well for optimum steam production.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Keeping hull drag low by having clean hull and propeller.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Not using an extra generator or power pack unless warranted. Aux engines to be used at optimum load and not run idle at low loads for standby.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Maintaining air filters clean so that internal combustion machinery develops full power.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Main engine rpm should be high enough for exhaust boiler to produce enough steam so that aux boiler is&nbsp;&nbsp;used to minimum.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">For better exhaust heat utilisation, wash ME turbocharger turbine and blower side regularly.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">ME jacket cooling water temperature should be maintained high enough and cooling in SW circuit to be optimum, for max FWG production.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">FWG to be regularly descaled for optimum FW production.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Automatic temp and viscosity controllers help.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Chief engineer to take Draw Diagrams of ME, to check for bad combustion. Excessive soot on the poop deck is a good indication.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Tankcleaning and steam pipelines and valves to be maintained in good condition, to prevent loss of hot water/ steam.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Avoid loss of heat to heated cargoes due to cold interface from SBT.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Ensure steam traps work and only hot water return to atmospheric condenser or boiler hot well. Avoid unnecessary burning of bunkers in boiler. On a long voyage ship may run out of bunkers.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Hot water calorifier to be used economically and in timely manner.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Keep boiler feed water temp as high as possible, to save on fuel.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Keep accommodation well sealed to prevent AC plant running continuously without cutting off,&nbsp;&nbsp;and engine room doors shut to prevent heat ingressing cool accommodation.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Defrost reefer chambers regularly.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Deck water ,deck air deck , hyd power to be put on only when necessary.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Whenever possible use common pumps for cooling water.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Put of galley hotplates , vent and equipment when not in use.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Tankcleaning to be planned in a optimum manner.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Electrical motors and bearings to be well maintained .<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; Ajit Vadakayil", "url": "https://www.blogger.com/profile/14410812789424637654", "image": {"url": "//4.bp.blogspot.com/-QSnd-Z8F7Kc/XFtPudWdwlI/AAAAAAABfq4/vxrkFOO7Iu8Mf6-OaPgw6FPpRDSmMgLdgCK4BGAYYCw/s35/capt%25252BajitC%25252Bvadakayil.JPG"}}, "replies": {"totalItems": "0", "selfLink": "https://www.googleapis.com/blogger/v3/blogs/3564735312144269387/posts/28740153165844547/comments"}}, {"kind": "blogger#post", "id": "1015645074617066508", "blog": {"id": "3564735312144269387"}, "published": "2010-12-16T10:02:00+05:30", "updated": "2010-12-21T13:28:08+05:30", "etag": "\"iHf3yWDE_geBgZ8U7rgZ_xuTeAQ/dGltZXN0YW1wOiAxMjkyOTE4Mjg4MDQ5Cm9mZnNldDogMTk4MDAwMDAK\"", "url": "http://ajitvadakayil.blogspot.com/2010/12/respiratory-filters-on-chemical-tankers.html", "selfLink": "https://www.googleapis.com/blogger/v3/blogs/3564735312144269387/posts/1015645074617066508", "title": "RESPIRATORY FILTERS ON CHEMICAL TANKERS --  CAPT AJIT VADAKAYIL", "content": "<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TQmU11us5uI/AAAAAAAACBQ/NdAuFO1JRSg/s1600/chm.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TQmU11us5uI/AAAAAAAACBQ/NdAuFO1JRSg/s1600/chm.jpg\" /></a></div><br />\nMost oil major vetting houses, nowadays discourage Annex 2 chemical ships from keeping respiratory filters on board--the reason touted being-- sailors don't know how to use it!<br />\n<br />\nHOW PATHETIC!<br />\n<br />\nThis means if some ignorant , untrained pretender 2nd officer does NOT know how to use ECDIS -- all ships in the world must be penalised, and ECDIS must be removed from all ships.<br />\n<br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"background-color: yellow;\">In your company if &nbsp;filters are banned--the parcel chemical master must make a strong protest by SMS system.&nbsp;</span><br />\n<br />\nThe \" Alices in wonderland \" ashore have no idea, what it takes to squeegee a cargo tank containing nauseating fish oil laden with vermin and viruses -- or how to clean up a bio accumulative spill in the manifold drip tray.<br />\n<br />\nHave the law makers ever tried to squeegee a hot slippery tank with SCBA sets? <br />\n<br />\n<i style=\"background-color: yellow;\">In any case SCBA sets are NOT meant for \"working\". The \" working time\" in IBC code refers to \" lung demand time\".</i><br />\n<i><br />\n</i><br />\n<i>These jokers will take a flight to the capital city of their country , if they have to fill up a application &nbsp;form in capital--- at sea we sailors are handicapped by such riff -raff &nbsp;sitting on important chairs ashore -- who have reached there by tilted playing fields NOT by merit.</i><br />\n<br />\nBack to business--<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TQmVmw8ExRI/AAAAAAAACBU/fOdUWuz2Ts4/s1600/images+%25281%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TQmVmw8ExRI/AAAAAAAACBU/fOdUWuz2Ts4/s1600/images+%25281%2529.jpg\" /></a></div><br />\nALWAYS STUDY THE INSTRUCTIONS ON THE USER INSTRUCTION SHEET.<br />\n<br />\nRespiratory filters are consumer goods and require no maintenance. They ensure good protection against gases and vapours , toxic particles or borth combined.<br />\n<br />\nChoose the type of filter as per the requirement.<br />\n<br />\nThe oxygen content should be atleast 19.5 %. &nbsp;Air purifying respirators must NOT be used to protect against H2S. &nbsp;Leave the work area immediately, if breathing becomes difficult or dizziness or other distress occurs, encouraging all others individuals too in the same area.<br />\n<br />\nExposure to an oxygen deficient atmosphere can result in unconsciousness, paralysis, brain damage or even death. Initial symptoms of oxygen deficiency are:<br />\nHeadache, Drowsiness, Nausea, Weakness, Dizziness, Deep or laboured breathing, Unconsciousness.<br />\n<br />\nWhen dust or aerosols are present , use anti-dust or gas \u2013dust combined filer.<br />\n<br />\nPARTICLE filers of inert matters, low toxic particles and bacteria/ virus are available in the market.<br />\n<br />\nGAS filers are available for\u2014<br />\nOrganic vapours with BP&gt; or &lt; 65 deg C<br />\nOrganic gases like chlorine , H2S , ammonia and SO2. You can combine various types in one filter. Note the one-way arrow printed on the body of the filer. Ensure that the seal is always present. The filters have an expiry date.<br />\n<br />\nThere are filters which can aDsorb at low, medium and high capacities.<br />\n<br />\nCrew with beards and deep scars at the sealing areas are at risk due to leaks.<br />\n<br />\nIf a filter is damaged or battered do not use it.<br />\n<br />\nThe duration os a anti-gas filer depends on the aDsorbsion capacity of the aDsorbent agent, concentration in contaminanat, RH of air, temperature and lung demand of the user.<br />\n<br />\nThe filer must be immediately replaced if you can smell the gas or vapour.<br />\n<br />\nAs far as particles filters are concerned , inhalation resistance indicates filter clogging. When breathing becomes difficult change the filer, though protection is still satisfactory.<br />\n<br />\nWhen the contaminant is toxic , it is recommended to use the filter only once.<br />\n<br />\nStore the filters fitted with their caps in a cold and dry space free of toxic vapours. Do not store outside the temperature range -20C to+50C, or with RH&gt;90%.<br />\n<br />\nDo not use the filter 6 months after the first opening, or as mentioned in the instruction sheet.<br />\n<br />\nFilter masks can be used only 3hrs in a working day.<br />\n<br />\nUse proper face masks when sweeping health hazardous cargoes like yellow grease ( crushed bone meal ), tallow etc.<br />\n<br />\nWhen removing a mask take care not to breathe in the contaminants on the external surface of the filter.<br />\n<br />\nFilter mask\u2014 full face with nose cup to prevent fogging, inhalation and exhalation valve<br />\n<br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: blue;\">Organic vapor cartridges are no use for inorganic vapors</span>.<br />\n<br />\nNever remove a mask before leaving the contaminated area.<br />\n<br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: blue;\">Filter protection must only be used against gases which has a distinctive smell and there is no lack of oxygen</span>. If you can smell gas it means the filter is saturated and is to be discarded.<br />\n<br />\nClass 1/ 1000ppm<br />\nClass2/ 5000 ppm<br />\nMark X/ low BP products<br />\n<br />\nWhen loading Carcinogenic, Toxic or Bioaccumulative cargoes, spot checks of vapor concentrations should be carried out with Draeger tubes, to ascertain is TLV-TWA are being exceeded, and if PPE like face filters or SCBA should be worn by watchkeepers.<br />\n<br />\nThe Vervey\u2019s tankcleaning guide gives the VP/TLV ratio--- anything more than one is dangerous requiring the use of Draeger tubes on deck. Epichlorohydrin is 17, Methanol is 0.46 (200/92)<br />\n<br />\nPersonnel directly involved in the disconnection of toxic chemical cargo hoses should wear suitable filters / respirators.<br />\n<br />\nPersonnel supervising the disconnection of cargo hoses should stand upwind of, and away from, the operation.<br />\n<br />\nWhen squeegeeing tanks at end of veg oil/ fats discharge , the portable vents must run -- oxygen content must be at least 19.5% for short time exposure ( 20% for longer time ) --use the 4 runner portable gas instrument to check for CO and H2S.<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TQmV0YXI0BI/AAAAAAAACBY/K--x0ebjWVk/s1600/download.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TQmV0YXI0BI/AAAAAAAACBY/K--x0ebjWVk/s1600/download.jpg\" /></a></div><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: blue;\">Fill up a risk assessment form when sailors, have to wear air filters, with SEVERITY and PERIOD OF IMPACT/ CERTAINTY on the matrix.&nbsp;</span>. This ensures that Chief officer or Master is involved in selecting the filter mask. <o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify; text-autospace: none;\"><span style=\"font-family: Arial, sans-serif; margin-bottom: 0in; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify; text-autospace: none;\"><span style=\"font-family: Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 10pt; line-height: 115%;\">If the cargo is not water soluble or reactive try to use sea water to stop leakage of chemical into sea. This ballast water contained in the tank is to be considered dirty ballast and must be processed accordingly.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify; text-autospace: none;\"><span style=\"font-family: Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 10pt; line-height: 115%;\">In case of toxic, or flammable cargo take appropriate precautions. <o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; mso-layout-grid-align: transferring the cargo to another ship, for sea cleaning, for stability and stress calculations etc.) <o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify; text-autospace: none;\"><span style=\"font-family: Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 10pt; line-height: 115%;\">Fix vessel\u2019s position on Chart and, if deemed necessary, broadcast navigational warnings. <o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; text-align: center;\"><a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TQjQmjHT_OI/AAAAAAAACAg/bzF0eEpe1D0/s1600/chm.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TQjQmjHT_OI/AAAAAAAACAg/bzF0eEpe1D0/s1600/chm.jpg\" /></a></div><br />\n<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><b style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 16.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">PROPYLENE OXIDE<o:p></o:p></span></b></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-top: 10.0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify; text-autospace: none;\"><b style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">In general the cargo temperature should be kept/ maintained below 25C. If the ambient temperatures are low cooling systems need not be run.<o:p></o:p></span></b></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><b style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">It is mandatory to have 100% emergency<u> </u>backup cooling capacity is required. The backup unit can be used ONLY if the the working unit has broken down.<o:p></o:p></span></b></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-top: 10.0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify; text-autospace: none;\"><b style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">A slow increase in temperature due to sun on deck can be kept in check by sprinkler system. A sudden unexplained increase in temperature is highly unlikely, but in case that happens it could be due to polymerization. The Ship Operator and company must be contacted immediately. Jettisoning of cargo may be the answer.<o:p></o:p></span></b></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-top: 10.0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify; text-autospace: none;\"><b style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Greedy charterers will try to use low ambient temperatures and keep ship at the borderline without cooling systems -- &nbsp;Master is the man on the spot and the best judge, about temperatures expected during the voyage .</span></b></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-top: 10.0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify; text-autospace: none;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">Propylene oxide , Butylene oxide and Mixtures of Propylene and Ethylene oxide containing upto 26% are all included under ALKYLENE OXIDE. They can only be carried on ships which have the chemical approved in the COF. <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>Ships that have never carried Alkylene oxide will be inspected by a surveyor under the CDI scheme, to verify compliance. Zinc based coatings are acceptable.</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-top: 10.0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Loading temperatures will NOT exceed:--<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-top: 10.0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">PO/ 25 C<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-top: 10.0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">BO/ 35 C<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-top: 10.0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">MO/ 20 C<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-top: 10.0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">If the ship does NOT have a refrigeration system with separate cooling SW lines and pumps , the tanks must have 6000 mm Aq pressure rating, unless the ambient temperatures are very low, and the BP of the chemical can never be breached. The ship must be able to provide high purity nitrogen pad during the entire transit. <o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-top: 10.0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Past 3 cargoes in the cargo tank earmarked should not have contained acids, alkalies, amines , ammonia or oxidizing substances. Review the USCG compatible chart for adjacent cargo . Cargo systems must be free of all residues of polymerization inhibitors such as TBC ( Tertiary Butyl Catechol ) , from prior cargoes of Vinvl Chloride Monomer, Butadiene, Isoprene or Styrene. A waterwash cannot effectively remove TBC, only a copius methanol spray wash can.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-top: 10.0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Master should request the specific product safety data sheet before commencement of loading. A product safety data sheet for Propylene Oxide must be posted .<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Used for making polyurethane foams, coatings, adhesives, fumigant, insecticide etc.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Recognised carcinogen<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Colorless liquid<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Sweet Ether-like odour above 200ppm <o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Marpol category /Y<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">SG/ 0.83<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Correction Factor 0.001248<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Cargo group/ Alkylene Oxide<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">CHRIS code/ POX<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">MP/ -104.4C<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">AH/ 30 deg C<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">VP at 20 deg C / <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>449 mm Hg<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">VP at 34.5 deg C / 760mm Hg<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Vapor density (air =1.0)/ 2<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Solubility in water at 20C/ 40.5%<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">An extremely reactive, flammable liquid with a wide explosive range. Ignited by heat, sparks or open flame. Flashback along vapor trail may occur. Fire or contamination may cause violent rupture of the tank.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">FP/ less than-29</span><span style=\"font-family: Symbol; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-char-type: symbol; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-symbol-font-family: Symbol;\"><span style=\"mso-char-type: symbol; mso-symbol-font-family: Symbol;\">\u00b0</span></span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">C<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Flammable limits/ 2.1% to 37%<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Autoignition temperature/ 465 deg C<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Nitrogen of high purity 99.9% N2<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>, with oxygen content &lt;0.05% ( 500 ppm )<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Massive water spray can extinguish small Propylene Oxide fires<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Personnel will not usually tolerate moderate or high vapor concentrations<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Will bum skin and eyes. <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>Diluted solution is more irritating than undiluted.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Very destructive on mucose membranes<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">If vapor inhaled, it will cause dyspnea ( difficulty in breathing ), pulmonary odema, headache, nausea, vomiting or loss of consciousness<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Irritation of eyes and respiratory tract. Overexposing will cause serious injury.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>Contact with uncovered skin produces frostbite. Ingestion by skin will cause serious illness or death.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Coughing, watering eyes, nausea, frostbitten skin.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Prolonged contact with skin causes frostbite burn. Smarting of skin and first-degree bums on short exposure; may cause secondary bums on lung exposure.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Soluble in water, Alchohol , Acetone, Benzene and Ether.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">In case of spillage use sand to absorb, not saw dust.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Polymerize violently on distillation or in the presence of catalysts such as nonoxidizing mineral acids, Sulfuric acid, Nitric acid, Organic acids, Caustics, Ammonia, Aliphatic amines, Alkanolamines and certain salts.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Stainless Steel,<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>Zinc Silicate Coatings are materials resistant to Propylene Oxide.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">USCG compatibility chart/16<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">During activities where the potential for exposure is high, like connection and disconnection, sampling and opening the tank after discharge for cleaning, the personnel involved should wear full personal protective equipment, which includes full eye, body, and respiratory protection<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-top: 10.0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify; text-autospace: none;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">All crew members should be advised about the hazards of the Propylene Oxide and be instructed to stay away from the deck area around the manifold during cargo operations. Appropriate warning signs should be posted at the gangway and around the deck also indicting that double skin and bottoms as well as cofferdams are inerted.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-top: 10.0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify; text-autospace: none;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Vessel ventilation systems drawing air from the weather deck area should not be used during all loading, discharging, and cleaning operations involving Propylene Oxide.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-top: 13.0pt; </span></span></span><!--[endif]--><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Cooling units to be test run .<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom: .0001pt; text-indent: -.25in;\"><!--[if !supportLists]--><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: Calibri;\"><span style=\"mso-list: Ignore;\">7.<span style=\"font: 7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span></span></span><!--[endif]--><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Ensure all tank pressure sensors are corrected for zero error.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom: .0001pt; </span></span></span><!--[endif]--><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Pressure gauges (if any sensors are faulty) to be installed on each tank.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom: .0001pt; text-indent: -.25in;\"><!--[if !supportLists]--><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: Calibri;\"><span style=\"mso-list: Ignore;\">9.<span style=\"font: 7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span></span></span><!--[endif]--><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Nitrogen generators to be test run\u2014or bottle bank to be ready.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom: .0001pt; </span></span></span><!--[endif]--><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">If additional Y-piece and reducer are used, position a stainless steel valve at the outside (to prevent spill from extra pipe space when disconnecting the shore hose).<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom: .0001pt; </span></span></span><!--[endif]--><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">All valves, piping and<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>tanks to be pressure tested .<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; margin-left: 0in; margin-right: 0in; margin-top: 10.0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-fareast-font-family: Calibri;\"><span style=\"mso-list: Ignore;\">12.<span style=\"font: 7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span></span></span><!--[endif]--><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">The deck sprinkler system to be tried out.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; margin-left: 0in; margin-right: 0in; margin-top: 10.0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo1; mso-pagination: none; tab-stops: list .25in; text-align: justify; text-autospace: none; text-indent: -.25in;\"><!--[if !supportLists]--><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: Calibri;\"><span style=\"mso-list: Ignore;\">13.<span style=\"font: 7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span></span></span><!--[endif]--><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Closed MMC sampling device to be tested.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; margin-left: 0in; margin-right: 0in; margin-top: 10.0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo1; mso-pagination: none; tab-stops: list .25in; text-align: justify; text-autospace: none; text-indent: -.25in;\"><!--[if !supportLists]--><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: Calibri;\"><span style=\"mso-list: Ignore;\">14.<span style=\"font: 7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span></span></span><!--[endif]--><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Use dedicated seamless stainless steelhoses or Hosta Flon (Teflon lined) hoses marked: \"For alkylene oxide transfer only.\"<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; margin-left: 0in; margin-right: 0in; margin-top: 10.0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo1; mso-pagination: none; tab-stops: list .25in; text-align: justify; text-autospace: none; text-indent: -.25in;\"><!--[if !supportLists]--><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: Calibri;\"><span style=\"mso-list: Ignore;\">15.<span style=\"font: 7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span></span></span><!--[endif]--><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Manifold drip trays to be cleaned and bottom covered with two inches fresh water.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; margin-left: 0in; margin-right: 0in; margin-top: 10.0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo1; mso-pagination: none; tab-stops: list .25in; text-align: justify; text-autospace: none; text-indent: -.25in;\"><!--[if !supportLists]--><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: Calibri;\"><span style=\"mso-list: Ignore;\">16.<span style=\"font: 7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span></span></span><!--[endif]--><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Check Teflon vapor return hoses and connections. <o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-top: 10.0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify; text-autospace: none;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">All tanks must be VISUALLY inspected for readiness first, <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>and then nitrogen purged to 2% oxygen level ( DOW needs lower level of 0.5% or 5000 ppm ). Double skin must be nitrogen purged to bring down oxygen content to 2% ( 20000 ppm ) , only then ship is load ready.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-top: 10.0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify; text-autospace: none;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Connecting the cargo hose must be supervised by Chief officer.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-top: 10.0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify; text-autospace: none;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Prior to loading the manifold and the tank area to be taped off and unauthorized personnel not allowed in this area. Post proper warning signs.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-top: 10.0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify; text-autospace: none;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">The pre-loading inspection includes; High level and overflow alarms testing, tank tightness, remote temperature accuracy check, tank pressure gauge, closed ullage device and safety equipment preparedness check. <o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-top: 10.0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify; text-autospace: none;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Before commencement of loading the piping system to be pressurized and tested for leaks, using Nitrogen.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-top: 10.0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify; text-autospace: none;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Under no circumstances must open ullaging/ sampling be done. First foot sample is a must in narrow mouth bottles with Polyseal caps. Loading cannot resume unless the results are received. Samples must be retained for 6 months.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-top: 10.0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify; text-autospace: none;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Ship's equipped with IGG can use the same for purging of void spaces and double bottoms.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-top: 10.0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify; text-autospace: none;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Adjacent cargo tanks must either be inerted, loaded with compatible cargo or ballasted.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-top: 10.0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify; text-autospace: none;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Double skin must be inerted or ballasted.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><u><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">IMMEDIATE AFTER LOADING</span></u><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-top: 13.0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify; text-autospace: none;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">For line clearing use Nitrogen.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-top: 13.0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify; text-autospace: none;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Cargo lines must not be allowed to be drained into the drip tray.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-top: 13.0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify; text-autospace: none;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Manifold , domes and valves o be sealed.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-top: 13.0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify; text-autospace: none;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Disconnecting the cargo hose must be supervised by the Chief Officer.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-top: 13.0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify; text-autospace: none;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">After loading is completed and ullaging, sampling is completed immediately reduce tank pressure to 1400 mm Aq and monitor if pressure holds steady.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-top: 13.0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify; text-autospace: none;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Start cooling units and run them for system function check, provided cargo level is sufficient <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span>in the tank.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-top: 10.0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify; text-autospace: none;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">In general the cargo temperature should be kept/maintained below 25C. &nbsp;If the ambient temperatures are low cooling systems need not be run.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-top: 10.0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify; text-autospace: none;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">It is mandatory to have 100% emergency<u> </u>backup cooling capacity is required. The backup unit can be used ONLY if the the working unit has broken down.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-top: 12.0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify; text-autospace: none;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Positive pressure between 700-1400 mm Aq must be maintained throughout the voyage.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-top: 12.0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify; text-autospace: none;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Observe and record tankwise cargo temperature/ pressure <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>every 4 hours. The carriage log will be attached to the surveyors report at Disport.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-top: 12.0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify; text-autospace: none;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Daily measure the Oxygen content in ballast tanks and void spaces surrounding the cargo tanks. Keep a slight overpressure in these spaces.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-top: 12.0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;\">Rise in Temperature means </span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>either the cooling units are not working or that the cargo may be reacting.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-top: 13.0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;\">If it is loss of cooling </span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">, change over to back up cooler. if possible, repair the inoperative cooler. The coolers must <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>never be removed from the tank loaded with Propylene Oxide. Watch the cargo temperature and tank pressure closely. Notify the Ship Operator and company.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-top: 10.0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify; text-autospace: none;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">A slow increase in temperature due to sun on deck can be kept in check by sprinkler system. A sudden unexplained increase in temperature is highly unlikely, but in case that happens it could be due to polymerization. The Chemical Operator must be contacted immediately. <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>Jettisoning of cargo may be the answer.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Loss of pressure means there are leaks.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><u><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">PRIOR TO DISCHARGE PREPARATIONS</span></u><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-top: 13.0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify; text-autospace: none;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Purge the pumps) cofferdam by N2 before commencement of pumping.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-top: 13.0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify; text-autospace: none;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Manifold drip trays to be cleaned and filled with 2 inches fresh water.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-top: 9.0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify; text-autospace: none;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">The tank pressure to be closely monitored and kept at positive pressure by nitrogen balancing.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify; text-autospace: none;\"><u><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">TANK WASHING<o:p></o:p></span></u></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-top: 6.0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify; text-autospace: none;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Without opening any butterworth ports take in a few cubic meters of fresh water into the tank from the manifold. Pump this water overboard at sea.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-top: 6.0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify; text-autospace: none;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Ventilate the tank .<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-top: 6.0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify; text-autospace: none;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">During the ventilation operation, all flammable/ toxic precautions must be taken. Crew members should be kept away from the area.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-top: 9.0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify; text-autospace: none;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Propylene Oxide vapors are heavier ( double ) than air and in certain weather conditions, Propylene Oxide vapor may concentrate above deck-level and travel a considerable distance along deck or enter into any other tank or spaces that may be left open.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-top: 9.0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify; text-autospace: none;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Propylene Oxide vapors are highly soluble in water, such that a water spray (Butterworthing) into a tank containing Propylene Oxide vapor may result in a rapid reduction of the tank interior pressure and COLLAPSE the tank. Use of inert gas is an acceptable method of purging cargo tanks for cleaning.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TQjQs01r2NI/AAAAAAAACAk/v3sYf-pOGWE/s1600/capt+ajit+vadakayil.JPG\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TQjQs01r2NI/AAAAAAAACAk/v3sYf-pOGWE/s1600/capt+ajit+vadakayil.JPG\" /></a></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-top: 9.0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify; text-autospace: none;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-top: 9.0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify; text-autospace: none;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">-------CAPT AJIT VADAKAYIL ( 28 YEARS IN COMMAND )<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-top: 9.0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify; text-autospace: none;\"><br />\n</div>", "author": {"id": "14410812789424637654", "displayName": "Capt.
