mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Encourage every crew member to talk about their mistakes, so all can learn from them. This is the way to build a winning team. Cargo work involves team work dynamics and is not a one man show.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><b><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Shipboard losses can be from--</span></b><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Evaporation via PV vents.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Deliberate retention for ulterior motives.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Excessive ROB due to high pour-point of cargo or pumping problems.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><b><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">\u2018On Paper Only \u2019 virtual losses : \u2013</span></b><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">In many shortage claims no actual loss has taken place but the amount of cargo has been overstated when loading and/or<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">understated when discharging.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">To avoid large vapour losses, is the Reid vapour pressure (RVP) of the cargo within the ship\u2019s PV capacity?<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Company policy often dictates the&nbsp;<i>filling limit</i>. 98% of a tank\u2019s capacity generally allows for cargo temperature to increase&nbsp;</span><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Arial, sans-serif;\">by 20\u00b0C - but the difference in temperature between northern Europe and the tropics often exceeds this figure. Imagine a cargo&nbsp;&nbsp;of Pentane loaded from LeHavre to US gulf.</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Ullages exceeding limits set out in the ship\u2019s stability book can lead to excessive free surface. This can cause sloshing,&nbsp;</span><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Arial, sans-serif;\">making&nbsp;<i>pressure/vacuum valves \u2018breathe\u2019</i>&nbsp;and resulting in vapour losses or \u2018boil off\u2019 of the lighter fractions of the cargo. This dynamic sloshing stress can cause structural failure and endanger the crew/ ship.</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Stowing volatile cargo next to heated cargo causes evaporation losses. Charterers should specify maximum&nbsp;<i>adjacent temperatures</i>.&nbsp;&nbsp;AH&nbsp;&nbsp;is an important spec on chemical tankers.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><i><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Chief officer must find out:--</span></i><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Number of shore tanks to be loaded from,&nbsp;&nbsp;the quantity, temperature and SG of cargo in each.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Whether there are any planned loading stops for shore tank changes.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Whether density is being expressed \u2018in air\u2019 or \u2018in vacuum\u2019<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Whether shore pipelines are full or empty, and details of any pipeline displacements planned.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Whether loading by gravity or shore pumps.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Whether pumps are displacement ( screw ) or non- displacement ( centrifugal ) . Topping up is easy with gravity loading and centrifugal pump loading as valves can be throttled. Only a non-displacement pump can tolerate the ship shutting valves while it is pumping.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">While in some trades the discharge port\u2019s out turn figures alone determine the amount of cargo delivered, in others they&nbsp;</span><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Arial, sans-serif;\">are still compared to the bill of lading figures provided by the loadport.</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Even if both terminals carry out their measurements diligently, each will (quite legally)&nbsp;<i>round off temperature and ullage&nbsp;</i></span><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Arial, sans-serif;\">readings in its favour, so differences are only to be expected. In the absence of a like-for-like comparison, the ship is the only common factor - and therefore the measurements taken on board are critical. The inspector must be accompanied at all times and his ullage measurements actively verified.</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><i><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Measurement errors</span></i><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">&nbsp;often result from commercial pressures. Remembering that, long after the immediate pressure has been forgotten, the ship will remain responsible for having ensured that the measurements were carried out correctly. Some owners&nbsp;</span><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Arial, sans-serif;\">employ cargo superintendents ( supercargo ) to relieve the pressure. If, in spite of all measures taken, an early departure procedure, for example, exposes the ship to any unwarranted liability, she must protest.</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Use of defective equipment-- frequently maintaining and checking ship\u2019s equipment - and arranging for&nbsp;<i>regular calibration</i>&nbsp;of electronic measuring devices by an agent approved by the manufacturer improper measurement technique--- doing homework, sharing experience around and encouraging everyone to talk about their mistakes, so all can learn from them.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Never permit the use of the terminal\u2019s measuring equipment on board. If measurements taken with the&nbsp;<i>inspector\u2019s equipment</i>&nbsp;differ from those taken with the ship\u2019s, propose that all measurements be taken with each, and both be sent for verification ashore afterwards.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">If the retro-fitted vapour lock valves required by electronic gauging equipment have changed the height and/or position of the ullage point, measurements taken through such valves must be corrected before use. This&nbsp;<i>Vapor lock reference measurement</i>&nbsp;( can be found in P@A manual ) should be posted in CCR bulkhead prominently.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><i><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">If the ship is pitching or rolling</span></i><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">, five measurements should be taken, withdrawing the tape as soon as it penetrates the surface of the cargo. The highest and lowest should be ignored and the middle three averaged. Weather and sea conditions should be logged.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">In the same conditions on inerted ships, or where electronic, closed gauging equipment is used, the probe should be withdrawn and lowered until three readings differ by no more than 5mm.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><i><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Taking cargo temperature</span></i><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">: The temperature of every cargo tank should be recorded separately.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><i><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Cargo temperature</span></i><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">&nbsp;may vary by 5 \u00b0C at different levels in the tank, so must be averaged from at least three readings -<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">top, middle and bottom. Some digital probes can measure at more frequent intervals<b>&nbsp;</b>A measurement error of 1\u00b0C can distort&nbsp;</span><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Arial, sans-serif;\">the volume calculation by +/-0.1%, depending on cargo density.</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><b><span style=\"color: white; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Checking cargo density</span></b><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Checking&nbsp;<i>cargo density</i>.&nbsp;Despite practical difficulties, it is best practice to make sure the density of the cargo is measured and compared with the figures supplied by the terminal.&nbsp;If the loading terminal measures densities in vacuum and the discharge&nbsp;</span><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Arial, sans-serif;\">port in air, the figures must be corrected to avoid an apparent loss .&nbsp;A difference of 0.0100 Kg/litre in cargo density can alter a VLCC\u2019s tonnage calculation by some 3,000 metric tonnes</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Allowing for&nbsp;<i>trim/ list</i>:&nbsp;&nbsp;Many loadport cargo measurement errors are caused by failing to make due allowance for trim and list. These should be based on draft readings whenever possible.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><i><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Free water</span></i><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">:&nbsp;&nbsp;The quantity of any free water detected must also be corrected for trim and list. Protest even small amounts, as there is likely to be more in suspension.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><i><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Cargo calculations</span></i><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">: Make sure all parties are using the same edition of&nbsp;<i>the ASTM Petroleum Measurement tables</i>&nbsp;for mineral cargoes. Make sure ASTM tables are NOT used for organic chemicals. If the surveyor insists , then make a remark . Ensure disport also uses the same tables.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Make sure the&nbsp;<i>contents of the ship\u2019s pipelines</i>&nbsp;are included in the calculations.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Sign the inspector\u2019s quantity report \u2018for ullages and temperatures only\u2019.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Apply the&nbsp;<i>vessel experience factor</i>&nbsp;(VEF).<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">If the ship\u2019s figures differ from the shore\u2019s, review the calculations.&nbsp;&nbsp;If the difference is confirmed, initiate the owner\u2019s standard procedure.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><i><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Cargo surveyor</span></i><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">:&nbsp;&nbsp;Accompany the inspector at all times, ensuring that he measures temperatures, ullages, densities, list and trim<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">accurately.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Ullaging active tanks regularly and comparing results with hourly shore discharge&nbsp;<i>rates</i>&nbsp;helps ensure that cargo is not being&nbsp;<i>misdirected / diverted&nbsp;</i>in the receiving terminal.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Monitoring air and sea temperature and sea state can provide valuable evidence in case of a subsequent dispute about the&nbsp;<i>pumpability&nbsp;</i>of the cargo. Most shore pipelines are not heated or lagged.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><i><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Stripping</span></i><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">&nbsp;&nbsp;The best way to avoid losses resulting from charter party freight retention clauses is to make sure the ship can&nbsp;</span><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Arial, sans-serif;\">demonstrate it did everything possible to discharge all the cargo. Provided it is within the ship\u2019s stress limits, the greater the trim aft, the better the drainage, especially with high MP and viscous cargoes.</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">When stripping&nbsp;<i>high pour-point&nbsp;</i>cargo: Maintain cargo at the recommended discharge temperature until the heating coils are about to be exposed start stripping as soon as cargo pumping stops. Protest any request from the shore to stop. If the stop is essential, continue stripping to an accumulation tank and resume cargo heating as soon as possible.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">When stripping&nbsp;<i>high vapour pressure</i>&nbsp;cargoes: Avoid operating pumps at excessive speed which increases vaporisation, causes cavitation and reduces suction. Increasing the pressure of inert gas in the cargo tank or increasing the back pressure on the pump can improve pumping performance.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><i><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Re-inspect</span></i><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">&nbsp;\u2018empty\u2019 tanks before declaring a grade finished.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><i><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">ROB determination:</span></i><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Additional cargo may have accumulated due to:<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Changes in list and trim<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Bulkhead, pipeline or valve leaks difficulty of calibrating bottom levels of tanks<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Blocked limber holes, on inner frame tanks<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Unmeasurable tank side clingage<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Uncertainty about the liquidity of bottom residues<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">It is always important to observe and log precisely how the inspector&nbsp;<i>measures ROB.&nbsp;</i>Ensure he surveys all the cargo tanks.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Make sure he takes great care reading sounding rods or bobs, to avoid the common mistake of overstating the liquid element of bottom residues because it has run down over the sediment as the rod is raised.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Ask him to take samples of the bottom residue, from more than one point in each tank if possible.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">If you suspect that the&nbsp;<i>samples&nbsp;</i>may be unrepresentative because of the tendency of less viscous material to flow more easily into the sampling device, ask the inspector to sample the more viscous material found in the pump mud box or the manifold when it is disconnected.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Urge that the&nbsp;<i>wedge formula</i>&nbsp;be applied only to the liquid element of the ROB, since it can be argued that there must be as much sediment under the liquid as there is in the dry parts of the tank.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Ensure that the tank dry certificate states that&nbsp;&nbsp;All&nbsp;<i>pipelines</i>&nbsp;are&nbsp;<i>stripped dry</i>. Do not allow the shore hoses to be disconnected until the inspector has signed a dry tank certificate, or a statement of ROB, that you agree with. If you dispute the inspector\u2019s figures, initiate company standard procedure.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Calculate the ROB independently, compare results with the inspector\u2019s and log any differences.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><b><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">CONTAMINATION:</span></b><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">In the contest against claims, as in today\u2019s competitive market place, only the best informed will win.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Approximately 45% of alleged shipboard contamination problems are, on investigation, found to be shore related.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><b><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Shoreside</span></b><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Residues of previous contents of storage tanks, lines and hoses.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Tank and line cleaning media, including water.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Other products, because of valve leakage or mis-operation or poor in-line blending.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Fresh water or impurities carried over from the manufacturing process.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Fresh water from leaking heating coils or tank roofs.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Salt water from leaking sub-sea pipelines.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><b><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Shipboard</span></b><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Residues of previous contents of ship\u2019s tanks, lines, pumps and hoses.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Dirty sounding and ullaging equipment.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Tank coating deficiencies.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Tank and line cleaning media, including water.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Other part cargoes, because of valve leakage, valve mis-operation or tank structural deficiency (e.g. bulkhead cracks).<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Other part cargoes\u2019 vapour via common inert gas systems.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Salt water from leaking tank hatch domes, butterworth ports , sounding pipes and vents.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Fresh water from leaking heating coils.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Copper leaching from alloys used to manufacture heating coils on CPP ships (e.g. alloy brass contamination of jet fuel).<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Is the tank coating suitable for the cargo? For example white wine needs stainless steel; epoxy is preferred for vegetable oils.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Some cargoes can permanently damage certain coatings, others make coatings soft for a while, during which time the&nbsp;range of cargoes they can tolerate is restricted. Refer to the&nbsp;<i>coating manufacturer\u2019s resistance lists.</i><o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">For multi-grade loadings, plan the use of pumps and pipelines to avoid or minimise commingling or downgrading. Ensure line displacements are calculated such as to avoid cross-contamination.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">If ullages are insufficient, cargo from one tank can slosh through a&nbsp;<i>common vent line</i>&nbsp;to contaminate non-compatible cargo&nbsp;in an adjacent tank, if the ship rolls or pounds.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">The vapours of one grade can put another grade out of specification, e.g. gasoline and kerosene or diesel, if the&nbsp;<i>VRS spools</i>&nbsp;are not disconnected.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Heat reduces the effectiveness of&nbsp;<i>inhibitors,</i>&nbsp;so avoid stowing inhibited cargoes adjacent to heated tanks.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">The Chief Officer must ascertain the following from the terminal representatives-&nbsp;<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">whether the shore pipeline is dedicated--details of any&nbsp;<i>shore pipeline displacements</i>&nbsp;planned number of shore tanks to be loaded from, &nbsp; and the quantity, temperature and density of cargo in each.&nbsp; Whether any loading stops are planned for shore tank changes, &nbsp; whether ship or shore is responsible - and how to stop in an emergency.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">If changes are to take place without stops, that the ship receive notification of every change for sampling purposes.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Whether the ship will be receiving two sets of samples from the shore tanks: one for the receiver, one for the shipowner<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">(if not, log that the request was made and refused)<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><i><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Cargo surveyor</span></i><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">:--<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Remember, an \u2018independent inspector\u2019 is independent in name only - expect him to give the ship\u2019s interests low priority, and&nbsp;make sure he is accompanied by an officer at all times.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">An experienced officer may well be more expert than the inspector, who is usually a non-marine person or even a ex-junior officer.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Tanks cannot be entered where local regulations insist on constant operation of the inert gas system but, whenever possible, make sure that the inspector checks every tank thoroughly.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">If the ship\u2019s pipelines have been drained, demonstrate this to him and ensure it appears on the inspection certificate.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Outside the chemical trade, tank inspections are often subjective so, if you do not agree with the inspector, try to reach a commercial solution \u2013 always faster and cheaper than a legal one.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">As soon as it becomes apparent that you cannot agree,&nbsp;<i>protest.</i><o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Sampling: Adopt a sampling procedure that satisfies the relevant authorities.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Make sure the ship has the right equipment, including clean bottles, seals and labels.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><i><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Label samples</span></i><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">&nbsp;with the following information:<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Ship\u2019s name,&nbsp;date and time<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Location,&nbsp;cargo name<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Operational status (e.g. \u2018after loading\u2019)<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Sample source (e.g. \u2018tank number...\u2019)<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Sample type (e.g. \u2018top\u2019; \u2018composite\u2019)<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Identity of sampler<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Seal number<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Make sure each sample is signed and sealed, preferably by the independent inspector. Note the particulars of every sample taken for the ship\u2019s purposes in a sampling log. Present the inspector with a list of samples drawn and retained by the ship for acknowledgement and signature.&nbsp;Require any party to whom a sample is handed over to sign a receipt for it.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Store samples in a secure space which is cool, well ventilated and not exposed to light.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Since the Hague Rules allow claims to be presented up to a year after the event, samples should not be disposed of until that&nbsp;period of time has elapsed.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Samples showing that the condition of the cargo did not change between loading and discharge provide the best defence&nbsp;against unfounded contamination claims.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">If the lab report is to be right, the sample must be right too - an inspector is as prone to error as the next man.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">The inspector must be accompanied at all times, to ensure that the sampling procedure satisfies the relevant authorities.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">If the inspector fails to do something he should, or does it wrong, point it out to him, and log anything he does not put right.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Log any faults with his equipment and any occasions when he borrows the ship\u2019s.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">As well as any samples he takes for the consignee, the receiver and his own firm, ask the inspector to take another set for&nbsp;the ship. If he refuses, note it in the log - and take your own.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Chief Officers should ensure they receive two sets of shore tank samples for each grade: one set for delivery to the&nbsp;receiver\u2019s agent; the other to be retained by the ship.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Asking the inspector to take starting samples at the manifold is the best way to detect contamination or commingling&nbsp;in shore lines.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Make sure first foot samples are taken to verify that the ship\u2019s lines are clean.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Discourage the inspector from subjecting them to visual analysis only, while loading continues.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Loading should be stopped while proper tests are carried out, particularly when the specification is critical.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">If the samples are off-test, advise the charterer without delay.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Even if tests reveal no problems, the ship must retain its duplicate samples in case of any later dispute.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Carry out spot checks at the manifold whenever practicable during loading, particularly after any shore stops and<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">preferably accompanied by the inspector or a representative of the terminal.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Accompany the inspector when he opens the sealed unit of any&nbsp;<i>composite sampler.</i><o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">After-loading samples should be taken from top, middle and bottom of each cargo tank.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">If the cargo is to be treated with an additive, the fact should be recorded on the bill of lading. Unless you are certain&nbsp;that the shipper and receiver have agreed to this taking place after loading, require any party proposing to do this to sign for&nbsp;receipt of a letter protesting the procedure - before he carries it out.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Make sure you receive a certificate in respect of cargoes that are inhibited.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">At the discharge port, in-line samples of each grade of cargo should be taken at the manifold:<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">-&nbsp;at the start of discharging<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">-&nbsp;once during every watch that the grade is being discharged<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">-&nbsp;during stripping<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">-&nbsp;If the inspector fails to take any of these samples, the ship should take its own.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">-&nbsp;Make sure the inspector samples any free water found, so that its source can be established.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">-&nbsp;Sampling gas oil bunker tanks after loading and before discharging helps defend against claims that cargo has been used as<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">bunkers.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Maintain a minimum of two-valve separation throughout the discharge of multiple grade cargoes. On chemical tankers, unnecessary spols are removed and blanked.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Valves should be sealed (if they were not sealed in the loadport) and the seals pointed out to the inspector and logged.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">If possible, leave seals in place until discharge is completed and ask the inspector to note the fact.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">The most easily contaminated grades should be&nbsp;<i>discharged first</i>, if possible. If any grade cannot tolerate contact with residues of the grade before, strip the cargo line. If necessary, flush the line with the second grade and re-strip - it is better to lose part of the cargo through downgrading than to contaminate all of it and the shore tank besides.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">A watch officer discovering contamination should:<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">-&nbsp;stop discharging the relevant cargo<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">-&nbsp;close that system\u2019s valves<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">-&nbsp;advise the Chief Officer, who advises the Master, who contacts the owner and his local P&amp;I correspondent.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">The Master should:<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">-&nbsp;sample the remaining cargo and request testing<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">-&nbsp;await instructions from the owner<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Crew must never try to conceal a operational error which may result in contamination. The sooner problems are identified, the less the owner\u2019s potential exposure.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; text-align: left;\"><span style=\"background: yellow; color: red; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Remember-- &nbsp;on chemical tankers ( unlike oil tankers ) we take manifold sample --WITHOUT opening the manifold valve--for obvious reasons.. &nbsp;</span><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TQg60qc1BLI/AAAAAAAAB8s/X_0tN-BC3wQ/s1600/capt+ajit+vadakayil.JPG\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TQg60qc1BLI/AAAAAAAAB8s/X_0tN-BC3wQ/s1600/capt+ajit+vadakayil.JPG\" /></a></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">CAPT AJIT VADAKAYIL ( 28 years in command )<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt; line-height: 115%;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"background-color: yellow;\"><br />\n</span></span></div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt; line-height: 115%;\">Pay attention to the size of portholes. It is no big secret that a sailor likes to have a large panoramic porthole , which gives a sense of freedom , rather than a pigeon hole opaque porthole.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><br />\n</div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt; line-height: 115%;\">Ensure the dining room and lounges are larger, more comfortable and better equipped with entertainment facilities, to encourage crew interaction and bonding.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><br />\n</div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt; line-height: 115%;\">Light management:-- Low intensity green light to improve alertness. Blue light makes you less sleepy sleepy and prevents lapses of concentration. It is understood that most modern radar screens allow you to choose the light shade.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><br />\n</div><div style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin: 0in;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt; line-height: 115%;\">Proper attached toilet facilities respecting need for privacy and storage space for personnel effects reduce stress and create a sense of well being.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both;
